       <article class="post-43247 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-entertainment-news" id="post-43247">
        <div class="row post-top large">
         <div class="entry-media-wrapper">
          <div class="entry-content-media" style="background-image: url(http://www.menzmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/matthew-and-camila-pic.jpg);">
          </div>
         </div>
         <!-- END .entry-media-wrapper -->
         <div class="entry-header-wrapper">
          <header class="entry-header">
           <h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">
            Matthew Mcconaughey  Matthew McConaughey: Gaining Weight Was Hard
           </h1>
           <!-- END .entry-title -->
           <div class="entry-meta clearfix">
            <div class="date updated">
             January 7, 2014
            </div>
           </div>
           <!-- END .entry-meta -->
          </header>
          <!-- END .entry-header -->
         </div>
         <!-- END .large-6.columns -->
        </div>
        <!-- END .row -->
        <div class="entry-content">
         <div class="post-side-share position-above" id="post-side-share-above">
          <div class="clearfix">
           <a class="icon icon-twitter icon_embed_tw" href="http://twitter.com/home/?status=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.menzmag.com%2Fentertainment%2Fentertainment-news%2Fmatthew-mcconaughey-matthew-mcconaughey-gaining-weight-was-hard%2F+-+Matthew+Mcconaughey+%26%238211%3B+Matthew+McConaughey%3A+Gaining+Weight+Was+Hard" target="blank" title="Twitter">
            <span class="share-network">
             Twitter
            </span>
           </a>
           <a class="icon icon-facebook icon_embed_fb" href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.menzmag.com%2Fentertainment%2Fentertainment-news%2Fmatthew-mcconaughey-matthew-mcconaughey-gaining-weight-was-hard%2F&amp;t=Matthew+Mcconaughey+%26%238211%3B+Matthew+McConaughey%3A+Gaining+Weight+Was+Hard" target="blank" title="Facebook">
            <span class="share-network">
             Facebook
            </span>
           </a>
           <a class="icon icon-google-plus icon_embed_gplus" href="https://plusone.google.com/_/+1/confirm?hl=en&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.menzmag.com%2Fentertainment%2Fentertainment-news%2Fmatthew-mcconaughey-matthew-mcconaughey-gaining-weight-was-hard%2F" target="blank" title="Googleplus">
            <span class="share-network">
             Google +
            </span>
           </a>
           <a class="icon icon-linkedin icon_embed_linkedin" href="http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&amp;url=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.menzmag.com%2Fentertainment%2Fentertainment-news%2Fmatthew-mcconaughey-matthew-mcconaughey-gaining-weight-was-hard%2F&amp;summary=Matthew+Mcconaughey+%26%238211%3B+Matthew+McConaughey%3A+Gaining+Weight+Was+Hard&amp;source=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.menzmag.com" target="blank" title="Linkin">
            <span class="share-network">
             Linkedin
            </span>
           </a>
           <a class="icon icon-comment icon_embed_comments" href="#comment" title="Comments">
            <span class="share-network">
             Comments
            </span>
           </a>
           <span class="arrow">
           </span>
          </div>
          <a data-flip-widget="flipit" href="https://flipboard.com">
           Add to Flipboard Magazine.
          </a>
          <script src="https://cdn.flipboard.com/web/buttons/js/flbuttons.min.js" type="text/javascript">
          </script>
         </div>
         <div class="clearfix" itemprop="articleBody">
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           <span style="color: #000000;">
            <a href="http://www.menzmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/matthew-and-camila.jpg">
             <img alt="Matthew Mcconaughey" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-43248" height="500" src="http://www.menzmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/matthew-and-camila.jpg" width="500"/>
            </a>
            Matthew McConaughey says it was harder for him to re-gain the weight he lost slimming for his acclaimed role as real-life
            <span id="more-43247">
            </span>
            AIDS sufferer Ron Woodroof in Dallas Buyers Club.
            <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
             <strong>
              Matthew McConaughey
             </strong>
            </span>
            found it harder re-gaining the weight he lost for Dallas Buyers Club than he did losing it. The 44-year-old actor underwent a crazy transformation for the physically demanding role as aids sufferer Ron Woodroof, shrinking from his ripped beach physique to a gaunt frail frame by losing around 50 pounds. Surprisingly, the Failure to Launch star admitted that he found returning to his original weight more difficult than dropping it.
           </span>
          </p>
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           <span style="color: #000000;">
            The Hollywood star  who is married to
            <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
             <strong>
              Camila Alves
             </strong>
            </span>
             told Hollyscoop: I gained 45 [pounds] of them back. The gaining was trickier than the losing. Its more fun, but its also trickier. The first big meal that you eat, your body remembers that it lived at 182 pounds and it wants to sprint back and you have to pull the reigns and go, Woah! We gotta take it easy. Its a marathon.
           </span>
          </p>
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           <span style="color: #000000;">
            Matthew  who has been receiving critical praise for the role and has received a Golden Globe nomination for Best Actor  was honoured with an award for his role in the film at the Palm Springs International Film Festival on Saturday (04.01.13) and is already being hotly tipped for an Oscar nomination. He said of the films success: It makes it that much more enjoyable to be here sharing it because we were the underdog from day one. Weve been the underdog for 20 years.
            <strong>
             -Contactmusic
            </strong>
           </span>
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
